<time>1481071558619< /time><rate>5</rate><Text>Carl is one of the most genuine individuals i have ever met. He as been mounting my tires for about a year and a half now and this evening i needed a new rear mounted. Had picked up a tire from another vendor - they failed to inform me that the tire was a decade old. Carl pointed out the manufacture date to me while we were chatting and decided it was still in decent enough condition to attempt to mount. Upon the mounting, large chunks of rubber began peeling away due to the brittle inner bead rubber area. At this point the tire was toast and a replacement was needed

Carl had a tire on hand and proceeded to mount, balance, and shake my hand telling me the tire was free due to his mess up with the other tire. After a short discussion in which i stated i could not accept such a generous offer for something that wasnt really is fault, we agreed on charging me dealer cost for the tire and a free mount and balance.

Carl has been willing to go above and beyond EVERY single time he and i have interacted. People like him are hard to find, plain and simple.

i ask that the biker community support him whenever they can and help keep an amazing person and a locally owned business open.</Text><pics>None</pics>< response>

< text>
A dump of a campground. We came on a weekend in August, so it was busy. Couldn't even use the restroom because they were so filthy. Trash EVERYWHERE! We at least cleaned up the mess others had left in our campsite. Dumpsters were full. No camp host. Very poorly managed. Park service should be ashamed of themselves. This is a place that people come to drink lots of beer, make lots of noise, then leave lots of trash lying around. After driving through other campgrounds along the Kern River, this seemed to be the norm. We would have been better off finding a good spot along the side of the road to camp and not paying the $20 a night for the site. On the plus side, it did have a good location with good river and swimming access. May be a better place to stay during the week when it's less busy.</text>

< Review>
The swimming is great.  The site is a disaster.  I spent the first 20 minutes picking up garbage.  There's a good deal of garbage at the river.  What really troubled me was a group of about 15 gentlemen who were leaving empties all over (glass and cans) and fishing lures right where kids were swimming.  They did this all day with total impunity.  They also stayed up partying until 5 with no resistance (to me that's nowhere near as bad as watching them trash our beautiful wilderness).

The guy running the camp came by when we first got there to make sure we had paid for the spot.  Some alcoholics can be identified by the degradation of their noses.  This guy is one of them.  After about 3pm he was nowhere to be found.  He didn't answer my knocks on his trailer door Sunday morning.  I was hoping to float the idea that if each one of those goons got a $1000 fine for littering, they could clean up the campground.< /Review>

<rating>5< /rating>< Review>
Stayed at this campground 6/10 through 6/12/2016.  If you're looking for a 5 star hotel who's looking to get fanned and a room with a bidet this ain't for you.  If you're looking for a good campground along the Kern River in the high desert with minimal shade this is for you.  Starting off, great access to river, no showers.  Toilets are stone outhouses with a simple seat and a big window you can see through so if you want extra privacy bring some tacks and a towel with you and tack that towel up for some extra privacy while handling your business.  They aren't great but I've seen much worse.  We were lucky this weekend because everyone on property was clean and picked up after themselves and in the toilets.  If you want a clean campground you pick up your crap, your dog's crap and co-exist with your neighbor's.  Great people were there to meet.  The campground itself is clean and nice.  Great views and you are right on the river.   Fire pits have a swing down grill plate and worked great.  I cooked chicken thighs, steak, roasted veggies and we did breakfast on them as well.  Water access is great, lots of faucets.  15 minute drive from town.  Would stay here again.

Lastly, the camp host was on-site and did ask a group who'd taken our parking spot to be kind and move (which they so kindly did).  He was friendly and kept a tidy camp ground.  Knowledgeable about the area and welcoming to our group of 8 people.<//Review>

< user>
102318800919908992194</user>
<username>Lindsey Harrison</username><Date>1533852385528<//Date><rate>4</rate>< review>
Bring extra trash bags and be prepared to pick up trash after people who dont care about keeping this place beautiful.  That's including down by the river. My husband and I filled three small trash bags.

The river was a perfect flow and made tubing really fun, if you were willing to hike up the river a little & tube down. Make sure you bring your river shoes! Be prepared for it to get crowded down by the water during the day. We met a very large family who were camping at Hospitals, a few campsites south of Gold Ledge, and apprently word of mouth gets around and Gold Ledge is the spot to go for the day to cool off and hang out. There is very little space at the "beach", so make sure you set all of your stuff up there the night before or at sunrise, or you will be sitting in the rocks.

The firepits at the camping spots were a neat plus. 17, 18 & 19 are camping spots facing eachother. This location would be perfect for multiple people wanting to camp together. Our family stayed at one of these spots and it definitely did not feel private. Also, curfew is not enforced. People were walking around way past 11pm and being inconsiderate of others trying to sleep.

This was a neat spot to camp. One fellow camper calimed it was one of the best spots to camp on Kern. I cannot agree with that. Our kids loved it & that is all that really matters. It was a little too crowded for my comfort and since it's up river, there is not as much wild life (bullfrogs, deer, foxes, birds, etc) or foliage. Bring a pop up or two. No shade.< /review>

<Text>Great Korean fried chicken and pizza restaurant. I don't know why they changed the name to Koko, but seems it's part of the Love Letter Pizza & Chicken chain restaurants. It's a medium sized restaurant, didn't seem very busy Tuesday lunchtime. Their specialties are Korean fried chicken and Korean style pizza, which has a stuffed crust with your choice of sweet potato, pumpkin, or cheese. They have various combos that include both pizza and chicken that you can get too.

GREAT
* Sweet and mild chicken - The whole chicken order was a good basketfull of delicious fried chicken. Each piece was well sized, crispy on the outside and juicy inside. Well complemented by the slightly sweet sauce.
* Sweet and spicy chicken - Spicy version of the above. Has a good kick.

GOOD

This is an excellent Korean hof that feels quite a bit like being back in Korea. Koko N Pizza is basically a Korean style bar, where the main event is drinking soju and beer, and there is some basic bar food offered to go with it. The fried chicken here is good. The pizza is fine, but it's great drunk food. What is really nice about this place is that the soju and beer are priced very well, and the staff provide very good service but are laid back. They have large tables that are good for big groups, and it's no problem if you get a bit loud and rowdy. This is a very good spot to keep the party going after some bbq!< /Review>

Well I used to be loyal to the local businesses I still am for the most part. But I'm sorry I've been going to Elkins for years, slowly the quality has gone down and as of 3-18-19 I will no longer stop to eat there. I was standing at the window to order for 5mins or more waiting for the girl to finish her cigarette (or phone call or maybe both). Anyways some other customers pulled up got out of their truck went inside as I'm waiting to order and finally the server came in washed her hands and passed me right up and started taking their order!
